## Concepts

### Level 0 - Foundational

#### Error

An error is a mistake or inaccuracy in texts, figures, or programs which can lead to unintentional consequences in output or results.

**Also known as:** Mistake, Inaccuracy

**Tags:** quality control, software, content accuracy

**Related:** Limitation of Liability, SAP

---

#### Limitation of Liability

Limitation of Liability is a legal clause that limits the amount or types of damages a party can claim in case of errors or damages resulting from the use of products or services.

**Tags:** legal, risk management, contracts

**Related:** Error, Trademark, SAP

---

#### Trademark

A trademark is a symbol, word, or phrase legally registered or established by use as representing a company or product.

**Also known as:** Registered Trademark, Unregistered Trademark

**Tags:** legal, intellectual property, business

**Related:** Limitation of Liability, SAP

---

#### SAP Fiori

SAP Fiori is a common design paradigm for SAP applications aimed at creating intuitive business apps accessible across all platforms and devices, guided by design principles such as role-based, responsive, simple, coherent, and delivering instant value.

**Also known as:** Fiori UX, Fiori

**Tags:** user experience, SAP, UX, enterprise software, User Interface, UX design, SAP UI, SAP user interface, SAP S/4HANA, UI technology, UI design, business applications, software design

SAP HANA is an in-memory database that combines OLTP (Online Transaction Processing) and OLAP (Online Analytical Processing) in a single system, simplifying data management and optimizing IT resource usage.

#### Stock Valuation

The process of assigning monetary value to stock items on the balance sheet according to their type and valuation method, reflecting the inventory's financial worth.

**Also known as:** Inventory valuation

**Tags:** SAP, Finance, Inventory, inventory management, accounting, material management, Materials Management, Inventory Control, financial valuation

**Related:** Segment (Financial Accounting), General Ledger Accounting (FI-GL)

---

#### Standard Ledger

A ledger type in SAP S/4HANA that records financial transactions according to one accounting principle and serves as the basis for other ledger types.

**Also known as:** Leading ledger, SAP standard ledger

**Tags:** SAP, Finance, General ledger, financial accounting, SAP S/4HANA, ledger, accounting principle

**Related:** SAP S/4HANA

---

#### Indicators (Special General Ledger Accounting)

**Tags:** SAP, Finance

**Related:** Indicator (Special General Ledger Accounting), Special General Ledger Accounting

**Tags:** SAP, Finance, Accounting

**Related:** Indicators (Special General Ledger Accounting)

#### Reversing documents

Reversing documents in SAP is the process of negating previously posted financial documents to correct errors or reflect changes in transactions.

#### Recurring journal entry

A recurring journal entry is a predefined accounting document that posts identical financial entries automatically at specified intervals over a period.

**Also known as:** Recurring entry, Recurring Entry Document

**Tags:** Finance, Accounting, Journal entries, SAP Finance, Automation, Financial Automation

**Related:** Posting accrual

#### Alternative Reconciliation account

An optional reconciliation account used in specific transactions to record different postings separate from the primary reconciliation account.

**Also known as:** Alternative reconciliation ledger account

**Tags:** Finance, Accounting, SAP

**Related:** Reconciliation account

---

#### Reconciliation account

A G/L account in SAP that collects line items posted to subledgers such as customers or suppliers, allowing payments to be posted to different accounts only by using special general ledger indicators or similar configurations.

**Also known as:** Reconciliation ledger account, Reconciliation G/L Account, Recon account

**Tags:** Finance, Accounting, SAP, Financial Accounting, GL Account, General Ledger, Subledger, master data, SAP S/4HANA, Accounting Account, SAP Financial Accounting, Subledger Accounting

**Related:** Alternative Reconciliation account, Line item

---

#### Reconcile GR/IR Accounts app

An SAP S/4HANA application used to create worklists, check items, and match open items to reduce open amounts in the goods receipt/invoice receipt clearing process.

**Also known as:** Goods Receipt/Invoice Receipt Reconciliation app, GR/IR Reconciliation App

**Tags:** SAP, Finance, Reconciliation, Application, SAP S/4HANA, accounting, software tool, financial process

**Related:** Reporting

---

#### Purchase order accruals

Process transferring purchase order data from materials management to the accrual engine, converting PO items into accrual items for calculation and posting.

**Tags:** Accounting, Accruals, Purchasing, Finance, Accrual Accounting, Procurement

#### Profit center maintenance

The ongoing process to update and manage profit center master data to accurately reflect organizational changes and controlling requirements.

**Tags:** Accounting, Controlling, Data Maintenance

**Related:** Profit center

---

#### Profit center hierarchy

A structured or flat organizational structure grouping all profit centers in a client, assigned to a controlling area to facilitate reporting, planning, and analysis.

**Tags:** Accounting, Controlling, Hierarchy, SAP, Organizational Structure, Profit Centers, financial accounting, SAP S/4HANA

**Related:** Profit center

---

#### Primary cost and revenue account

The main general ledger accounts used to record primary costs and revenues in financial accounting.

**Tags:** Accounting, Cost Accounting, Revenue

**Related:** Profit center

#### Posting schema

The framework defining the structure and lines included in accrual postings, including line-item types and symbolic accounts for account independence.

**Tags:** Accounting, Posting, Finance, Accrual Posting

**Related:** Posting period variant

---

#### Posting period variant

A configuration element assigned to company code and ledger that defines allowed posting periods differentiated by account type and period intervals.

**Also known as:** Posting period variant in SAP, Period Variant

**Tags:** Accounting, Fiscal Periods, financial accounting, configuration, posting periods, SAP S/4HANA, SAP, period control, SAP configuration

**Related:** Posting schema, Release approval path

---

#### Range (Posting key)

The numerical sequence or limits within which posting keys are defined and valid for certain types of postings.

**Tags:** Accounting

**Related:** Posting key

---

#### Conflicting field status

A condition in posting where the field status definitions cause conflicts preventing successful posting or requiring resolution.

**Tags:** Accounting, Posting

**Related:** Posting key

---

#### Account type (Posting key)

The classification of accounts (such as vendor, customer, or asset) that a posting key applies to for accounting entries.

**Tags:** Accounting

**Related:** Posting key

---

#### Posting key

A two-digit SAP financial accounting code that specifies the type of account to be posted (such as customer, vendor, or general ledger account) and whether the posting is a debit or credit.

**Also known as:** Transaction Posting Key, Posting Key Code, Posting Code, Posting Keys

**Tags:** Accounting, Posting, financial accounting, transaction coding, SAP, SAP S/4HANA, SAP Configuration, Accounting Posting, Finance, Document Posting, General Ledger, Financial Posting, document processing

**Related:** Account type (Posting key), Range (Posting key), Conflicting field status

---

#### Posting deferral

The accounting process of postponing the recognition of revenues or expenses to a later period, opposite to accrual posting.

**Tags:** Accounting, Deferrals

**Related:** Posting accrual

---

#### Journal (Posting accrual)

The specific general ledger or subledger journal where accrual postings are recorded.

**Tags:** Accounting, Journal Entry

**Related:** Posting accrual

---

#### Automatic reversal (Posting accrual)

A process by which an accrual posting is automatically reversed in a subsequent accounting period to avoid duplication of expenses or revenues.

**Tags:** Accounting, Accruals

**Related:** Posting accrual

#### Periodic physical inventory

A type of physical inventory where all stocks are counted at once on the balance sheet date, with warehouse movements blocked during counting.

**Also known as:** Annual Inventory

**Tags:** Inventory Management, inventory, materials management, stocktaking method

**Related:** Physical inventory

---

#### Cycle counting

An inventory counting method where stocks are counted at regular, configurable intervals during the year, typically used for fast-moving items.

**Tags:** Inventory Management, inventory, materials management, stocktaking method

**Related:** Physical inventory

---

#### Continuous physical inventory

A stock counting method where inventory is continuously counted throughout the fiscal year, ensuring each material is counted at least once annually.

**Tags:** Inventory Management, inventory, materials management, stocktaking method

**Related:** Physical inventory

---

#### Physical inventory

A business process involving physical counting and matching of actual stock with inventory records, usually conducted annually as a legal requirement.

**Also known as:** Stocktaking, Inventory Count, Inventory Counting

**Tags:** Inventory Management, Accounting, Operations, warehouse management, Materials Management, Inventory Control, Closing Activities, audit

**Related:** Continuous physical inventory, Cycle counting, Periodic physical inventory

---

#### Definition (Payment term)

The formal description and rules pertaining to payment terms within an accounting system, defining due dates and conditions.

**Tags:** Accounting, Payments

**Related:** General Ledger Accounting (FI-GL)

---

#### Day limit

The last valid day in a month by which an invoice must be dated for a specific payment term to apply, allowing multiple rules with different day limits per payment term code.

**Tags:** Accounting, Payments, SAP S/4HANA, Finance, Payment Terms

---

#### Default baseline date

The automatically assigned baseline date used in payment processing when no specific baseline date is provided.

**Tags:** Accounting, Payments

**Related:** General Ledger Accounting (FI-GL)

---

#### Baseline date

The reference date from which payment terms and due dates are calculated in payment processing.

**Tags:** Accounting, Payments

---

#### Account type (Payment term)

Classification of account involved in the payment term, such as vendor or customer accounts, influencing payment processing rules.

**Tags:** Accounting, Payments

---

#### Payment methods

Predefined procedures or channels through which payments are executed, defined at both country and company code levels with associated keys, descriptions, and configurations.

**Also known as:** Pymt Meth.

**Tags:** Accounting, Payments, Finance, SAP, Payment Processing, financial accounting, master data

---

#### Payment block reasons

Specific causes or justifications for placing a payment or invoice under a payment block, such as discrepancies or compliance issues.

**Tags:** Accounting, Payments, payment process, financial accounting, SAP S/4HANA, payment processing, accounting control, finance

---

#### Passive document split

The automatic SAP document splitting occurring without user configuration, such as payment clearing an invoice where the system splits entries automatically.

**Tags:** Accounting, Document Management, SAP, document splitting, process

**Related:** Payment run

---

#### Parked document

An incomplete SAP document assigned a system-generated document number saved for later completion or approval; visible in some reports and processes.

**Also known as:** Parked Journal Entry

**Tags:** Accounting, Document Management, SAP Financial Accounting, SAP S/4HANA, Finance

**Related:** Post Incoming Invoices app, Manage Journal Entries app

---

#### Parallel valuation

An accounting technique allowing multiple valuations of the same asset or liability in parallel to comply with different accounting standards or purposes.

**Tags:** Accounting, Valuation, Parallel Accounting, finance, SAP S/4HANA

**Related:** Parallel accounting

---

#### Ledger approach (Parallel accounting)

A method of parallel accounting that involves maintaining multiple ledgers to reflect different accounting principles or valuation methods.

**Tags:** Accounting, Parallel Accounting

**Related:** Parallel accounting

---

#### Accounts approach (Parallel accounting)

A method of parallel accounting where separate sets of accounts are maintained in the general ledger for different accounting principles.

**Tags:** Accounting, Parallel Accounting

**Related:** Parallel accounting

---

#### Parallel accounting

Parallel accounting, also called parallel valuation, refers to the process of maintaining and reporting financial transactions according to multiple accounting principles simultaneously, often necessary for multinational companies.

**Also known as:** Parallel accounting using G/L accounts, Parallel Valuation, Multiple Accounting Principles

**Tags:** Accounting, General Ledger, financial accounting, SAP S/4HANA, accounting principles, multinational, accounting methods, financial reporting, Accounting Method, SAP, finance, ledgers

**Related:** Accounts approach (Parallel accounting), Ledger approach (Parallel accounting), Parallel valuation

---

#### Overdue Receivables app

An application to monitor and manage customer receivables that have passed their due date for payment.

**Tags:** Accounting, Receivables Management, Software

**Related:** SAP Fiori, Dunning Interval in Days

---

#### Outgoing payment

A financial transaction where funds are disbursed from a company, such as payments to vendors or other third parties.

**Tags:** Accounting, Payments

#### Deferral

**Also known as:** Deferred accounting, Deferred Expense, Deferred Revenue

**Related:** General Ledger Accounting (FI-GL)

#### Data Archiving

**Also known as:** Archive Management, Archiving, Archive, Data Storage Management

**Tags:** data management, storage, compliance, Database Management, Data Lifecycle, sap finance, SAP S/4HANA, system performance, Financial Accounting, SAP

**Related:** Data Aging, SAP Information Lifecycle Management

---

#### Data Aging

A database management technique that moves older or less frequently accessed data from SAP HANA’s in-memory storage (hot data) to slower, traditional disk storage (cold data) to optimize memory use and cost.

**Also known as:** Information Aging

**Tags:** data management, database, performance, Database Management, SAP HANA, Data Lifecycle, SAP S/4HANA, system optimization, Financial Accounting, SAP, Performance Optimization

**Related:** Data Archiving, SAP HANA technology

---

#### Indirect quotation

#### Cold Data (Historic Partition)

Data that has been aged out from the in-memory hot partition and stored on traditional disk-based storage, accessible but with slower retrieval times.

**Also known as:** Historic Partition

**Tags:** SAP HANA, Data Storage

**Related:** SAP HANA In-Memory Database, SAP HANA technology

---

#### Hot Data (Current Partition)

The partition in SAP HANA that holds current and frequently accessed data in-memory for fast processing.

**Also known as:** Current Partition

**Tags:** SAP HANA, Data Storage

**Related:** SAP HANA In-Memory Database, SAP HANA technology

---

A database management system that stores data primarily in RAM (memory) for faster data processing and retrieval compared to traditional disk-based storage.

**Related:** Cold Data (Historic Partition), Hot Data (Current Partition), SAP HANA technology

#### Simulation Run

#### Lowest-Value Valuation Method

An inventory valuation method where assets are valued at the lower amount between cost and market value, applied using delta logic which considers changes from previous valuations.

**Also known as:** Lower of Cost or Market

**Tags:** Accounting, Inventory Valuation, Valuation Methods

**Related:** SAP S/4HANA

---

#### Carryforward

An accounting procedure that transfers account balances from one fiscal year to the next, with balance sheet accounts carrying over their closing balance as the new opening balance and profit and loss accounts resetting to zero.

**Also known as:** Fiscal Year Carryforward, Balance Carryforward

**Tags:** Accounting, Financial Closing, Ledger Management, SAP Finance, Year-End Process, fiscal year-end, financial reporting

**Related:** Balance Carryforward Activities, General Ledger Accounting (FI-GL)

**Related:** Dunning Process

---

#### Customer Items Due By

The due date limit up to which customer open items are evaluated during payment runs; if left blank, the payment run posting date is used as the due date.

**Tags:** Payment Process, Finance, SAP S/4HANA

**Related:** Payment Proposal Run

---

#### Docs Entered Up To

The cutoff date for documents to be evaluated for payment; any invoice with a posting date later than this date is excluded from payment runs.

**Tags:** Payment Process, Finance, SAP S/4HANA

**Related:** Payment Proposal Run

---

#### Posting Date

The date the system uses to post the reversal of a document; when reversing in the same period, the original posting date is used, while for closed periods, the current date is typically entered.

**Also known as:** Accounting Date, Document Posting Date

#### Currencies Allowed (Payment Method)

#### Separate Payment for Each Reference

#### Exchange Rate Differences

The differences arising due to fluctuations in currency exchange rates between the time an invoice is posted and payment is made; the payment program can be configured to calculate and post these differences.

**Tags:** Finance, Currency Exchange, SAP

**Related:** Foreign Payments / Foreign Currency Payments, General Ledger Accounting (FI-GL)

#### Max. Cash Discount

---

#### Outgoing Payment with Cash Discount From

The minimum discount percentage rate at which the system will post a payment early to receive a cash discount; discounts below this rate are ignored and payment is made at net due date.

**Tags:** Finance, SAP, Cash Discount

**Related:** Max. Cash Discount, Grace Period (Tolerances Days for Payable), Manage Automatic Payments App

---

#### Grace Period (Tolerances Days for Payable)

The allowable number of days by which a payment's cash discount period or net payment period can be exceeded to permit delayed payment without penalty.

**Also known as:** Tolerance Days for Payable

**Tags:** Finance, Payment Terms, SAP

**Related:** Outgoing Payment with Cash Discount From, Manage Automatic Payments App

#### Residual Item

#### Partial Payment

#### Time-Dependent Tax (TDT) Calculation

#### Transaction FTXP

---

#### Gross Amount (Tax Base)

A tax base calculation method where tax is calculated on the full posted amount regardless of discounts, with adjustments made additionally in a separate step.

**Tags:** tax calculation, finance

**Related:** Tax Base Amount, General Ledger Accounting (FI-GL)

---

#### Net Amount (Tax Base)

A tax base calculation method where tax is calculated on the posted amount after subtracting relevant discounts.

**Tags:** tax calculation, finance

**Related:** Tax Base Amount, General Ledger Accounting (FI-GL)

---

#### Tax Base Amount

The amount on which tax is calculated, which can be defined by law as either the net amount (posted amount minus discounts) or gross amount (full amount regardless of discounts).

**Tags:** taxation, tax calculation, finance

**Related:** Gross Amount (Tax Base), Net Amount (Tax Base), General Ledger Accounting (FI-GL)

---

#### Account Key

A setting within a tax procedure in SAP S/4HANA used to maintain account determination, informing the system which accounts should be posted for tax transactions.

**Tags:** SAP configuration, accounting, tax accounting

**Tags:** taxation, finance

#### Ledger Approach

A method for implementing parallel accounting in SAP S/4HANA where separate ledgers represent different accounting principles, allowing simultaneous valuation and reporting.

**Also known as:** Ledger-Based Parallel Valuation, New General Ledger approach, Ledger-Based Approach

**Related:** Accounts Approach, Special General Ledger Accounting

---

#### Accounts Approach

A parallel valuation method in SAP S/4HANA where valuation differences are handled via separate general ledger accounts within a single ledger, avoiding duplication in the chart of accounts.

**Also known as:** Accounts-Based Parallel Valuation, Parallel Accounting Using G/L Accounts, Account-Based Approach

**Related:** Ledger Approach, Special General Ledger Accounting

---

#### P - Line Items with Technical Numbers / No Deletion Possible

An extension ledger type supporting predictive accounting, where journal entries have technical numbers without document numbers and must be reversed rather than deleted.

**Also known as:** P Extension Ledger

**Related:** Extension Ledger Types

#### S - Line Items with Technical Numbers / Deletion Possible

An extension ledger type used for simulation purposes where journal entries have technical numbers, allowing direct deletion.

**Related:** Extension Ledger Types

---

#### Standard Journal Entries

A type of ledger posting saved with document numbers in the standard ledger; these cannot be deleted directly but must be reversed if changes are needed.

**Also known as:** Standard Ledger Journal Entries

**Tags:** SAP S/4HANA, Accounting, Ledger Management, Journal Entry

#### Offsetting account

A general ledger account designated to balance out legacy data transfer postings, ensuring that transfers are accounted for without causing discrepancies in the financial statements.

---

#### Takeover date

The cutoff date defined during legacy data transfer marking the last period closed in the legacy system; data up to this date is taken as legacy values, afterwards SAP calculates values natively.

**Also known as:** Legacy system cutoff date

**Tags:** data migration, SAP, asset accounting

**Related:** Legacy data transfer with Microsoft Excel

---

#### Company code status

A parameter that defines whether a company code is set to allow data migration activities within the SAP system.

**Tags:** SAP, organization, settings

**Related:** Dunning Company Code, Dunning Area

---

A tool provided by SAP for migrating data into SAP S/4HANA systems using predefined templates and automated validation tools to streamline the data transfer process.

**Also known as:** Migration cockpit

**Tags:** SAP, migration, tool

**Related:** Transaction LTMC, XML templates, SAP ERP, Asset transfer methods, Compatibility views, Migration preparation (Asset Accounting)

Payment program configuration involves setting options sequentially such as defining company codes, payment methods at country and company code levels, paying company codes, and bank determination to automate payment processing.

**Tags:** SAP S/4HANA, financial accounting, configuration

---

#### Foreign Currency Payment Clearing

When a payment in foreign currency clears an invoice exactly in that currency but results in a local currency variance due to exchange rate differences, SAP posts the difference to profit or loss accounts automatically.

**Tags:** SAP S/4HANA, financial accounting, currency management

**Related:** Payment Differences, General Ledger Accounting (FI-GL)

---

#### Payment Differences

Payment differences occur when the amount received differs from the invoiced amount, which can be managed in SAP by options such as partial payments or residual items.

**Tags:** SAP S/4HANA, financial accounting, receivables management, payment processing, accounting

**Related:** Post Incoming Payments App, Foreign Currency Payment Clearing, General Ledger Accounting (FI-GL)

---

The Post Incoming Payments app in SAP facilitates recording customer payments against invoices, with options to manage payment differences such as partial payments or residual items.

**Tags:** SAP Fiori, financial accounting, receivables

**Related:** Payment Differences, SAP S/4HANA

#### Negative Posting Reversal

A type of document reversal in SAP which creates line items opposite to the original posting (debit reverses credit and vice versa), effectively negating the original document's effects.

#### In-Memory Database

An in-memory database stores all data in a computer's RAM, enabling significantly faster read and write speeds compared to disk-based storage.

**Also known as:** RAM-based database

**Related:** SAP HANA technology

#### Intervals in Posting Periods

Three separate periods controlling different posting permissions: Interval 1 for normal operative periods, Interval 2 for special previous year periods, Interval 3 for controlling-related postings.

**Also known as:** Posting Period Intervals

**Tags:** financial accounting, period management, SAP S/4HANA

**Related:** Account Types in Posting Period Management, Authorization Group (AuGr), General Ledger Accounting (FI-GL)

---

A user group assignment in SAP controlling posting permissions to specified posting periods and account ranges for journal entries.

**Also known as:** Posting Authorization Group

**Tags:** security, financial accounting, SAP S/4HANA

**Related:** Intervals in Posting Periods, General Ledger Accounting (FI-GL)

---

Categories of accounts used to define period controls in SAP, including Assets (A), Customers (D), Suppliers (K), Materials (M), General Ledger Accounts (S), and All Accounts (+).

**Also known as:** Account Group Types

**Tags:** financial accounting, posting periods, SAP configuration

**Related:** Intervals in Posting Periods, General Ledger Accounting (FI-GL)

#### Incorrectly Assigned Accounts

Accounts assigned incorrectly to financial statement nodes, such as profit and loss accounts assigned to balance sheet nodes or vice versa, requiring review and correction.

**Also known as:** Misassigned Accounts

**Tags:** financial accounting, SAP S/4HANA, financial statement version

**Related:** Financial Statement Version Checks

---

#### Nonassigned Accounts

Accounts that are not included in the financial statement version structure, sometimes intentionally as in parallel accounting scenarios.

**Also known as:** Unassigned Accounts

**Tags:** financial accounting, SAP S/4HANA, financial statement version

**Related:** Financial Statement Version Checks

---

#### Accts Assigned to 1 Side Only

Accounts assigned exclusively to either debit or credit side in financial statement version nodes, potentially causing placement issues if the opposite balance occurs.

**Also known as:** Accounts Assigned One Side Only

**Tags:** financial accounting, account assignment, SAP S/4HANA

**Related:** Financial Statement Version Checks

---

#### Debit Balance

A debit balance in an account indicates that the debits exceed the credits, reflecting an asset or expense increase.

**Also known as:** Debit Side Balance

**Tags:** accounting, financial statements, accounting basics

---

#### Credit Balance

A credit balance in an account indicates that the credits exceed the debits, reflecting a liability, equity, or revenue increase.

**Also known as:** Credit Side Balance

**Tags:** accounting, financial statements, accounting basics

---

**Related:** Retirement Amount (Asset Retirement), Classic Asset Accounting

An option during asset retirement where you directly input the numeric amount to reduce the asset's value accordingly.

**Related:** Percentage Method (Asset Retirement), Classic Asset Accounting

#### Partial Sale (Asset Retirement)

An asset retirement method allowing a specific quantity or fraction of an asset to be sold, with corresponding value adjustments using amount or percentage methods.

**Also known as:** Partial Asset Retirement, Partial Disposal

**Tags:** Asset Accounting, Asset Retirement, SAP S/4HANA

**Related:** Revenue Account for Asset Sale, Partial Scrapping

**Also known as:** Asset Sale Revenue Account

---

#### Settling AUC Line Items

The process of transferring costs from Assets Under Construction (AUC) line items to final assets, triggering capitalization.

**Also known as:** Settlement of AUC

**Tags:** Asset Accounting, Capitalization, SAP S/4HANA

**Related:** Valuated Goods Receipt, Classic Asset Accounting

---

#### Nonvaluated Goods Receipt

A goods receipt process where the asset is not updated, and no capitalization occurs at goods receipt; asset values are posted later at invoice receipt.

**Also known as:** Non-Valuated GR

**Tags:** Procurement, Asset Capitalization, SAP S/4HANA, Inventory Management, Asset Acquisition

**Related:** Valuated Goods Receipt, General Ledger Accounting (FI-GL)

---

#### Valuated Goods Receipt

A goods receipt process that posts the asset at the goods receipt value, capitalizing the asset before the invoice is received.

**Also known as:** Valuated GR

**Tags:** Procurement, Asset Capitalization, SAP S/4HANA, Inventory Management, Asset Acquisition

**Related:** Nonvaluated Goods Receipt, Settling AUC Line Items, General Ledger Accounting (FI-GL)

---

#### Default Document Type

Predefined document types maintained in asset transaction types that are used automatically in postings unless manually overridden.

**Also known as:** Default Posting Document Type

**Tags:** SAP S/4HANA, Asset Transactions, Configuration

**Related:** Revenue Account for Asset Sale

---

#### Partial Scrapping

A process of retiring part of an asset's value or quantity without fully deactivating or removing the asset from the company records.

**Tags:** Asset Accounting, Asset Retirement

**Related:** Partial Sale (Asset Retirement), Fully Depreciated Assets

#### Fully Depreciated Assets

Assets that have reached the end of their depreciation schedule but remain active in company reports because they are still recorded in the system.

**Also known as:** Fully Depreciated Fixed Assets

**Tags:** Asset Accounting, Depreciation

**Related:** Partial Scrapping

#### SAP Simple Finance 1503

#### Universal Ledger

A financial accounting component introduced in SAP Simple Finance that consolidates all accounting data into a single table, simplifying financial processes and reporting in SAP S/4HANA.

**Also known as:** Universal Journal

**Tags:** SAP S/4HANA, financial accounting, data simplification

**Related:** SAP Simple Finance 1503

---

#### Compatibility views

Virtual views created by SAP to replicate obsolete or removed database tables dynamically, allowing legacy programs to continue running without modification during SAP S/4HANA migration.

**Also known as:** Compatibility layer views, Compatibility Views in SAP HANA

**Tags:** SAP S/4HANA, migration, backward compatibility, SAP HANA, database views, compatibility, SAP, database compatibility, legacy support

**Related:** SAP S/4HANA migration cockpit

---

#### Index tables

Tables used to speed up query performance by indexing key columns, commonly used in legacy systems for reporting but removed in SAP HANA due to its high-speed direct queries on line-item tables.

**Also known as:** Indexing tables

**Tags:** database, SAP HANA, performance optimization

**Related:** Aggregation tables

---

#### Aggregation tables

Database tables that store pre-calculated summary data, such as totals, to speed up reporting but can be removed in SAP HANA where totals are calculated on the fly from line items.

**Also known as:** Aggregate tables

**Tags:** database, SAP HANA, data modeling

**Related:** Index tables, Difference Between Data Aging and Data Archiving

---

#### Useful Life Maintenance Levels for Data Aging

Useful life for documents related to data aging can be maintained at various organizational levels within a company code to specify retention and aging policies.

**Also known as:** Useful Life of Documents, Data Aging Maintenance

**Tags:** Data Aging, Financial Document Management, SAP Configuration

**Related:** SAP Information Lifecycle Management

---

#### Difference Between Data Aging and Data Archiving

Data aging frees up memory space and allows retrieval of aged data for analysis, whereas data archiving permanently removes data from the database to reduce system load.

**Also known as:** Data Aging vs Archiving, Data Lifecycle

**Tags:** Data Management, SAP S/4HANA, Archiving vs Aging

**Related:** Aggregation tables

---

#### Deleting General Ledger Account and Chart of Accounts Relationship

Deleting a general ledger account for a company code does not remove it from the chart of accounts, as deletion is limited to company code-specific assignments rather than global account definitions.

**Also known as:** GL Account Deletion, Chart of Accounts

**Tags:** Financial Accounting, SAP Configuration, General Ledger

**Related:** Cross-Company Code Document, General Ledger Accounting (FI-GL)

---

**Also known as:** Validation Rules, Substitution Rules

#### Parked Documents

Parked documents are financial documents temporarily saved in the system that can trigger workflow processes, though they are not included in financial statements until posted.

**Also known as:** Document Parking

**Related:** Document Parking Workflow, Held Documents, Park General Journal Entries App

---

#### Held Documents

Held documents are journal entries or financial documents that have no document number assigned and can be incomplete, preventing them from triggering workflows or appearing in financial statements.

**Also known as:** Document Holding

**Tags:** Financial Document Management, SAP Workflow, Accounting

**Related:** Parked Documents

#### Balance confirmation

#### Accounts payable/accounts receivable regrouping

An accounting process that reorganizes payables and receivables on the balance sheet to conform with accounting standards, including moving debit or credit balances and transferring balances if reconciliation accounts change.

**Also known as:** AR/AP Regrouping, A/P and A/R Regrouping

**Tags:** accounting, financial statements, receivables, payables, Financial Closing, financial reporting, regrouping

#### Discrepancy resolution

**Also known as:** Solve discrepancies

**Tags:** accounting, reconciliation, problem-solving

**Related:** Reconciliation

---

#### Reconciliation

The process of ensuring that two sets of records (usually the balances of two accounts) are in agreement and any differences are identified and resolved.

**Also known as:** Account reconciliation

**Tags:** accounting, finance, process

**Related:** Discrepancy resolution, Reconciliation status, Matching algorithms, Accounts payable/accounts receivable regrouping, Balance confirmation

#### Passing Score for C_TS4FI_2020 Exam

The passing score for the C_TS4FI_2020 exam is 59%, which corresponds to correctly answering at least 48 out of 80 questions.

**Also known as:** Pass Rate, Pass Percentage

**Tags:** Certification Exam, Assessment Criteria

**Related:** C_TS4FI_2020 Exam

#### Multiple-selection Question (Type 2)

A multiple-selection question of type 2 requires selecting exactly three correct answers from five given options.

**Also known as:** Multiple-selection (3 of 5)

**Tags:** Exam Format, Assessment

**Related:** C_TS4FI_2020 Exam

#### Multiple-selection Question (Type 1)

A multiple-selection question of type 1 requires selecting exactly two correct answers from four given options.

**Also known as:** Multiple-selection (2 of 4)

**Tags:** Exam Format, Assessment

**Related:** C_TS4FI_2020 Exam

---

#### Multiple-choice Question

A multiple-choice question requires the exam taker to select one correct answer from several options, typically four in the SAP certification context.

**Also known as:** MCQ, Single-Answer Question

**Related:** C_TS4FI_2020 Exam

**Tags:** exam security, assessment

**Related:** Certification Exam

#### Question Bookmarking

The practice of marking questions that are uncertain during an exam to allow quick revisiting after completing other questions for efficient review.

**Also known as:** Flagging Questions

**Tags:** exam technique

**Related:** Certification Exam

---

#### No Penalty for Wrong Answers

A feature of SAP certification exams where incorrect answers do not deduct points, encouraging candidates to answer all questions and guess when unsure.

**Also known as:** No Negative Marking

**Tags:** exam policy

---

#### Exam Time Management

The strategy of allocating and using the given exam time efficiently, such as not rushing, spending approximately two minutes per question, and revisiting uncertain questions with time left.

**Also known as:** Time Management During Exam

**Tags:** exam strategy, time management

**Related:** Certification Exam

#### Balance Sheet Values by Account App

#### Standard Price

A fixed valuation price set for materials to value inventory uniformly, often used for work-in-process and finished goods stock.

**Tags:** valuation method, stock pricing, accounting

**Related:** Finished Goods (FG), Work-in-Process (WIP) Materials, SAP S/4HANA

---

#### Moving Average Price (MAP)

A valuation method that calculates the average cost of inventory items after each purchase or production run to provide an updated stock value.

**Also known as:** MAP

**Tags:** valuation method, stock pricing, accounting

**Related:** Raw Materials, Supplies, and Consumables (RSC), General Ledger Accounting (FI-GL)

---

#### Finished Goods (FG)

Products completed through the manufacturing process, produced in-house, and usually valuated at a standard price for stock valuation purposes.

**Also known as:** FG

**Tags:** stock types, manufacturing, inventory valuation

**Related:** Standard Price, SAP S/4HANA

---

#### Work-in-Process (WIP) Materials

Materials partially completed within the manufacturing process, also known as semifinished goods, typically valuated at standard price and capable of analytic breakdown on the balance sheet if customized.

**Also known as:** Semifinished Goods, WIP

**Tags:** stock types, manufacturing, inventory valuation

**Related:** Standard Price

---

#### Raw Materials, Supplies, and Consumables (RSC)

Stock categories typically purchased from suppliers and commonly valued using the moving average price (MAP) method.

**Also known as:** RSC

**Tags:** stock types, inventory, valuation methods

**Related:** Moving Average Price (MAP), General Ledger Accounting (FI-GL)

---

#### Posting Journal Entry

A detailed accounting document representing the clearing run, where the value posted is calculated from the price and quantity of materials, reflecting the financial impact of transactions.

**Also known as:** Journal Posting

**Tags:** accounting, SAP S/4HANA, financial documents

**Related:** Balance Sheet Values by Account App, Accrual/Deferral Journal Entry

---

#### Machine Learning Service in SAP Business Technology Platform

**Also known as:** ML Service in SAP BTP

**Tags:** machine learning, SAP Business Technology Platform, automation, accounting process

**Related:** Goods Receipt/Invoice Receipt Account Clearing

The accounting document that confirms the receipt of an invoice from a supplier for goods or services provided.

**Also known as:** IR

**Tags:** accounts payable, invoice processing, accounting documents

#### Goods Receipt

The confirmation document indicating that goods ordered have been physically received into inventory.

**Also known as:** GR

**Tags:** procurement, inventory management, accounting documents

#### Three-Step Reconciliation Procedure

A standard procurement process involving purchase order, goods receipt, and invoice receipt to ensure material and invoice data consistency.

**Also known as:** Procurement Reconciliation

**Tags:** procurement, materials management, accounting process

**Related:** Goods Receipt/Invoice Receipt Clearing Account

---

#### Goods Receipt/Invoice Receipt Clearing Account

A special ledger account used to post differences between received goods quantities and invoiced quantities during procurement processes.

**Also known as:** GR/IR Clearing Account

**Tags:** accounting, procurement, clearing account

**Related:** Three-Step Reconciliation Procedure, Balance Sheet Adjustment Account, Changed Reconciliation Account Option

---

#### Changed Reconciliation Account Option

A system option that reports all items of a changed reconciliation account using the new account from a selected key date during regrouping or reporting.

**Tags:** accounting, reporting, configuration

**Related:** Goods Receipt/Invoice Receipt Clearing Account

---

#### Value Adjustment Key

A configurable key that determines the percentage applied for flat-rate individual value adjustments.

**Tags:** accounting, value adjustment, configuration

**Related:** Special General Ledger Accounting

---

#### Special G/L Indicator

A classification tag used in general ledger transactions to identify special postings, such as for value adjustments (default type E for individual adjustment).

**Also known as:** Special General Ledger Indicator

**Tags:** accounting, ledger, posting

**Related:** Special General Ledger Accounting

---

#### Strict Lowest Value (Valuation Method)

A stricter valuation approach that posts adjustments only if the new value is lower than the current holding.

**Tags:** accounting, valuation, method

**Related:** Lowest Value Principle (Valuation Method)

---

#### Lowest Value Principle (Valuation Method)

A valuation approach where postings are made only if the valuation is worse than the original, with reversals made dependent on delta logic.

**Also known as:** Lower of Cost or Market

**Tags:** accounting, valuation, method

**Related:** Always Evaluate (Valuation Method), Strict Lowest Value (Valuation Method)

---

#### Always Evaluate (Valuation Method)

A valuation method that posts all differences regardless of whether they improve or worsen value; delta logic ensures valuation is not reversed.

**Tags:** accounting, valuation, method

**Related:** Lowest Value Principle (Valuation Method)

---

#### Delta Values

The differences in valuation amounts posted during multiple executions within a valuation period, representing changes since the last posting.

**Also known as:** Valuation Delta, Delta Posting

**Tags:** accounting, valuation, posting

**Related:** Valuation Posting Transactions

---

#### Valuation Posting Transactions

Accounting processes during valuation involving posting adjustments for exchange rate changes, automatic reversals in the following period, and posting delta values for multiple executions.

**Also known as:** Valuation Transactions, Valuation Postings

**Tags:** accounting, valuation, posting

**Related:** Valuation Run, Delta Posting Logic (Currency Valuation), Valuation Loss Account, Valuation Gain Account, Delta Values, Exchange Rate Difference Realized Accounts

---

#### Special Simulation Ledger

A dedicated ledger that captures simulation run data for analysis without impacting legal financial valuations.

**Tags:** accounting, ledger, valuation

**Related:** Special General Ledger Accounting

---

#### Update Run (Valuation)

A valuation run mode that executes real postings of foreign currency valuation results to the general ledger.

**Tags:** Finance, Accounting, Currency Valuation, System Process

**Related:** Valuation Run

---

#### Simulation Run (Valuation)

A valuation run mode that simulates posting results to preview the outcome without creating actual financial postings.

**Tags:** Finance, Accounting, Currency Valuation, System Testing

**Related:** Valuation Run

---

#### Test Run (Valuation)

A valuation run mode where no actual postings occur, used to verify calculations and configuration without affecting ledgers.

**Tags:** Finance, Accounting, Currency Valuation, System Testing

**Related:** Valuation Run

---

#### Exchange Rate Difference Realized Accounts

Profit & loss accounts used to post realized exchange rate differences when open items are finally cleared.

**Tags:** Finance, Accounting, General Ledger, Currency Valuation

**Related:** Valuation Posting Transactions

---

#### Balance Sheet Adjustment Account

A clearing account used to post valuation differences for reconciliation accounts (customer and supplier), as differences are not posted to individual sub-accounts.

**Tags:** Finance, Accounting, General Ledger, Currency Valuation

**Related:** Closing Activities in Receivables and Payables, Goods Receipt/Invoice Receipt Clearing Account

---

#### Valuation Gain Account

General ledger account defined to record gains arising from foreign currency valuation due to favorable exchange rate differences.

**Tags:** Finance, Accounting, General Ledger, Currency Valuation

**Related:** Valuation Posting Transactions

---

#### Valuation Loss Account

General ledger account defined to record losses arising from foreign currency valuation due to exchange rate differences.

**Tags:** Finance, Accounting, General Ledger, Currency Valuation

**Related:** Valuation Posting Transactions

---

Customizing setting that controls whether valuation postings automatically reverse monthly or are accumulated without reversal.

**Tags:** Finance, Accounting, Currency Valuation, System Configuration

**Related:** Valuation Posting Transactions

---

#### Exchange Rate Determination

Configuration determining which exchange rate types and sources are used for currency valuation postings.

**Tags:** Finance, Accounting, Currency Management

#### Valuation Procedure

Specific rules within a valuation method that define the timing and conditions for evaluating exchange rate differences, such as the lowest-value approach.

**Tags:** Finance, Accounting, Currency Valuation

#### Automatic Postings

#### Periodic Posting

**Tags:** Finance, Accounting, Accrual Accounting, Posting Types

#### Opening Posting

A posting type where the complete amount is posted on an accrual account at the beginning of the period.

#### Multiple Valuations

The practice of maintaining different sets of accounting values simultaneously to comply with various accounting standards or internal managerial needs.

**Tags:** Accounting Concept, Finance

**Related:** Account Sets

---

#### Period Accounting Method

An accounting approach that groups financial results by accounting periods rather than by cost of sales, resulting in a different cost and revenue breakdown but identical financial results.

**Tags:** Accounting Method, Financial Accounting

**Related:** General Ledger Accounting (FI-GL)

---

#### Financial Result

The net outcome of accounting processes reflecting profit or loss, which remains the same regardless of whether the cost of sales or period accounting methods are used, differing only in cost and revenue breakdown.

**Tags:** Accounting Concept, Financial Reporting

**Related:** General Ledger Accounting (FI-GL)

---

#### Clearing Account

An account used in SAP document splitting to post balancing clearing lines, ensuring zero balance per account assignment during document splitting.

**Also known as:** Clearing GL Account, Intercompany Clearing Account

**Tags:** Accounting Account, SAP S/4HANA, Financial Accounting, SAP, accounting, document splitting, cross-company transactions

**Related:** General Ledger Accounting (FI-GL)

---

#### Negative Reversal Posting

An accounting process where a negative amount is posted on the same debit or credit side as the original entry to maintain unchanged total debit/credit balances after an incorrect posting.

**Also known as:** Negative Posting

**Tags:** Accounting Process, SAP S/4HANA

**Related:** Document Reversal Process

---

#### Document Reversal Process

A procedure for reversing accounting documents where the posting date and reversal reason must be defined, and the reversal document type depends on the original document while the document date matches the original.

**Also known as:** Document Reversal

**Tags:** Accounting Process, SAP S/4HANA, Financial Accounting

**Related:** Negative Reversal Posting

---

#### Changeable Fields in Document Header

Only the document reference and document header text fields can be changed directly in SAP document headers; other changes require reversing and reposting the document.

**Tags:** SAP, Finance, Document Management

**Related:** Field Status Priority, General Ledger Accounting (FI-GL)

---

#### Posting Date and Period Determination

The posting date in SAP determines the accounting period for a document; postings are disallowed to closed periods except during special posting periods whose posting dates must be in the fiscal year's last period.

**Tags:** SAP, Finance, Period Management, Document Posting

**Related:** Special Posting Periods

---

#### Segment Requirement for Document Posting

A configuration in SAP where the segment field is made mandatory, preventing document posting without segment assignment and generating an error if missing.

**Tags:** SAP, Finance, Document Posting, Configuration

**Related:** General Ledger Accounting (FI-GL)

---

#### Tax Code Definition (FTXP Transaction)

Tax codes are defined by country using transaction FTXP in SAP to assign tax percentage rates per tax type and determine tax relevance of general ledger accounts.

**Also known as:** FTXP Transaction

**Tags:** SAP, Finance, Tax Configuration

---

#### Maximum Exchange Rate Deviation

A company code global setting in SAP that defines the allowable deviation in exchange rates during postings, unrelated to maximum tax amount.

**Tags:** SAP, Finance, Currency, Configuration

**Related:** General Ledger Document Posting

---

#### Currency Types

Categories used in SAP S/4HANA to record different monetary values in line-item tables, such as company code currency, document currency, and global currency, each serving specific accounting and legal requirements.

**Tags:** SAP, Finance, Currency, financial accounting, SAP S/4HANA

---

#### Special Posting Periods

Additional posting periods (like 13, 14, 15, 16) in SAP allowed within a fiscal year for adjustments and corrections, requiring posting dates in the last period.

**Tags:** SAP, Finance, Period Management

**Related:** Posting Date and Period Determination

---

#### Extension Ledger Group Assignment

---

#### Account Sets

Sets of accounts created to handle valuation differences when accounting according to multiple principles, used only when necessary.

**Tags:** SAP, Finance, Accounting, Master Data

**Related:** Multiple Valuations

---

#### Standard Ledger Assignment

A new standard ledger is not assigned to any company code automatically; the assignment must be completed manually during or after ledger creation.

**Tags:** SAP, Finance, Ledger, Accounting

**Related:** General Ledger Accounting (FI-GL)

---

#### Local Chart of Accounts Assignment

The assignment of a local chart of accounts to a company code is one-to-one, where one local account corresponds to a single operational chart of accounts account.

**Tags:** SAP, Finance, Accounting, Localization

---

#### Secondary Cost Accounts

Accounts used exclusively for transfer postings in controlling with zero balance for a company code, where debits are offset by credits on other secondary accounts; formerly known as secondary cost elements.

**Also known as:** Secondary Cost Elements

**Tags:** SAP, Controlling, Accounting, finance, cost accounting

**Related:** General Ledger Document Posting

---

#### Field Status Priority

The hierarchy controlling field behavior in SAP document entry, where 'Suppress' has the highest priority followed by 'Display', 'Required', and 'Optional'.

**Tags:** SAP, Finance, Field Configuration

**Related:** Changeable Fields in Document Header, General Ledger Accounting (FI-GL)

---

#### Group Account

A group account is defined at the chart of accounts level and is required when a group chart of accounts is assigned, representing consolidated accounts for reporting.

**Tags:** SAP, Finance, Accounting, Consolidation

**Related:** Chart of accounts

---

#### Indicator Blocking Assignments

An indicator that blocks accounts in the chart of accounts from being assigned to a company code, without affecting previously assigned accounts or postings.

**Tags:** SAP, Finance, Accounting, Master Data

**Related:** Special General Ledger Accounting

---

#### Account Number Length

The maximum length of an account number is defined by the chart of accounts, but the account group can limit this further by specifying a number range.

**Tags:** SAP, Finance, Accounting, Master Data

**Related:** Account Group

---

#### Country/Local Chart of Accounts

A country or local chart of accounts is a chart of accounts adapted to meet country-specific accounting standards, assigned to a company code.

**Also known as:** Local CoA

**Tags:** SAP, Finance, Accounting, Localization

**Related:** Chart of accounts

---

#### Operational Chart of Accounts

The required chart of accounts that contains accounts used for actual transactions and is assigned to the company code in global parameters.

**Also known as:** Operational CoA

**Tags:** SAP, Finance, Accounting, Chart of Accounts, Financial Accounting

**Related:** Chart of accounts

---

#### Account-based CO-PA

Account-based CO-PA is a profitability analysis method where characteristics are treated as additional account assignments to profit and loss accounts, allowing detailed reporting in financial accounting.

**Tags:** controlling, profitability analysis, SAP S/4HANA

**Related:** Profitability Analysis (CO-PA), General Ledger Accounting (FI-GL)

---

#### Profitability Analysis (CO-PA)

Profitability analysis is a controlling functionality in SAP that evaluates market segments according to revenues and costs, available in costing-based or account-based types.

**Also known as:** CO-PA

**Tags:** controlling, financial analysis, SAP S/4HANA

**Related:** Account-based CO-PA, General Ledger Accounting (FI-GL)

---

#### Secondary Cost Elements

Secondary cost elements represent internal allocations and cost transfers between controlling objects and are created as secondary cost general ledger accounts in SAP.

**Tags:** controlling, internal accounting, SAP S/4HANA

**Related:** Primary Cost Elements

---

#### Primary Cost Elements

Primary cost elements are general ledger accounts linked to management accounting that represent costs or revenues originating outside the controlling area and are used for cost tracking.

**Tags:** controlling, management accounting, SAP S/4HANA

**Related:** Secondary Cost Elements

---

#### Operating Chart of Accounts

The operating chart of accounts is the set of general ledger accounts used for management accounting and controlling purposes, requiring alignment between controlling area and company codes.

**Tags:** general ledger, controlling, SAP S/4HANA

**Related:** General Ledger Accounting (FI-GL)

---

#### Standard Period Accounting

Standard period accounting classifies expenses based on their origin such as personnel costs or depreciation, differing from cost of sales accounting but yielding the same total operating results.

**Tags:** financial accounting, cost accounting

**Related:** General Ledger Accounting (FI-GL)

---

#### Hierarchy Nodes

Hierarchy nodes are textual elements that represent levels within a profit center hierarchy, used to organize profit centers in SAP.

**Tags:** financial accounting, organizational structure, SAP S/4HANA

**Related:** Financial Statement Item Hierarchy

---

#### Company ID

A company ID is an identifier assigned to a company within the business partner master record to facilitate intercompany transactions.

**Tags:** master data, financial accounting, SAP S/4HANA

#### New Value Method (Asset Transfer)

A transfer method that capitalizes the new asset at a manually entered revenue amount instead of transferring the original historic or net book values.

**Tags:** asset accounting, transfer methods

**Related:** Transfer Method, Net Method (Asset Transfer), Gross Method (Asset Transfer)

---

#### Net Method (Asset Transfer)

A transfer method where the net book value (historic cost minus accumulated depreciation) of the sending asset is transferred to the receiving asset.

**Tags:** asset accounting, transfer methods

**Related:** Transfer Method, New Value Method (Asset Transfer), Gross Method (Asset Transfer)

---

#### Gross Method (Asset Transfer)

A transfer method where the historic acquisition and production cost values of the asset are transferred to the new asset in full.

**Tags:** asset accounting, transfer methods

**Related:** Transfer Method, New Value Method (Asset Transfer), Net Method (Asset Transfer)

---

#### Acquisition (Asset Transfer Context)

The posting made in the receiving company code to record the asset acquisition during an intercompany transfer.

**Tags:** asset accounting, posting

**Related:** Transfer Method

---

#### Retirement (Asset Transfer Context)

The posting made in the sending company code to remove the transferred asset from its asset registry during an intercompany transfer.

**Tags:** asset accounting, posting

**Related:** Asset Sale

---

#### Retirement with Revenue

An asset retirement scenario where the asset is retired through sale, generating revenue which is distributed to the selected assets in the retirement worklist.

**Tags:** asset accounting, asset retirement

**Related:** Retirement without Revenue, Retirement Worklist

---

#### Retirement without Revenue

An asset retirement scenario where the asset is retired without generating revenue, typically scrapping, and processed via the retirement worklist.

**Tags:** asset accounting, asset retirement

**Related:** Asset Scrapping, Retirement with Revenue, Retirement Worklist

#### Cash Discount

#### Cross-Company-Code Postings

#### Assets Under Construction (AUCs)

**Related:** Classic Asset Accounting

---

#### Low-value assets (LVAs)

**Also known as:** LVAs

**Tags:** asset management, accounting, depreciation

**Prerequisites:** LVA asset classes

**Related:** Asset Balances Report

#### Integration of Controlling with the General Ledger

An SAP S/4HANA feature where controlling and financial accounting share the same line-item table ensuring that postings in controlling are simultaneously posted to the general ledger for unified reporting.

**Also known as:** Manual Accrual Process

**Tags:** SAP, Accruals, Accounting Process, Accounting, Accrual Accounting

**Prerequisites:** Manual Accruals Customizing (SAP IMG ACAC Component)

**Related:** General Ledger Accounting (FI-GL)

---

#### Revenue Reporting

Revenue reporting is the accounting practice of recognizing revenues in the fiscal periods in which they are earned rather than when cash is received.

**Tags:** Accounting, Financial Reporting

**Prerequisites:** Accrual

**Related:** General Ledger Accounting (FI-GL)

---

#### Expenditure Reporting

Expenditure reporting refers to recording expenses in the appropriate fiscal period to reflect accurate financial performance and compliance.

**Tags:** Accounting, Financial Reporting

**Prerequisites:** Accrual

**Related:** General Ledger Accounting (FI-GL)

---

#### Profit & Loss (P&L) Account Carryforward

During carryforward, P&L accounts' balances are transferred to retained earnings in the master record, resulting in zero balances at the start of the new fiscal year.

**Also known as:** P&L Account Carryforward

**Tags:** Accounting, Profit & Loss Statement, SAP Finance

**Prerequisites:** Balance Types (Debit or Credit)

---

#### Balance Sheet Account Carryforward

In carryforward, balance sheet accounts transfer their closing balance from the previous fiscal year directly as the opening balance in the new fiscal year.

**Tags:** Accounting, Balance Sheet, SAP Finance

**Prerequisites:** Balance Types (Debit or Credit)

---

#### Account Assignment to Financial Statement Items

The allocation of general ledger accounts to the lowest-level nodes in a financial statement version hierarchy to enable proper financial reporting.

**Also known as:** Account Mapping

**Tags:** SAP, Financial Statements, Configuration

**Prerequisites:** Financial Statement Item Definition

---

#### Credit posting

An accounting entry that increases liability, equity, or revenue accounts or decreases asset or expense accounts, marked by posting keys such as 50 in SAP S/4HANA general ledger accounting.

**Tags:** financial accounting, posting key, SAP S/4HANA

**Prerequisites:** Posting key ranges and account types

---

#### Debit posting

An accounting entry that increases asset or expense accounts or decreases liability or equity accounts, marked by posting keys such as 40 in SAP S/4HANA general ledger accounting.

**Tags:** financial accounting, posting key, SAP S/4HANA

**Prerequisites:** Posting key ranges and account types

---

#### Migration Cockpit

**Related:** Manual Data Migration

---

#### Acquisition with Automatic Offsetting

An asset acquisition method where the asset is capitalized before receiving the invoice, involving debit to the asset and credit to an offsetting account, which is later balanced when the invoice is posted.

**Tags:** Accounting, Asset Acquisition, SAP S/4HANA, Posting Method

**Prerequisites:** Fixed Assets

**Related:** Asset Clearing Account

---

#### Purchase Order (PO)

A formal buying document used to request goods or services, which in asset acquisitions links to asset account assignment with category 'A' to enable capitalization.

**Tags:** Procurement, SAP S/4HANA, Materials Management

**Prerequisites:** Purchase Requisition

---

#### Clearing Document

A document created to balance and clear one or more open items in an account without changing the account’s overall debit or credit balance.

**Also known as:** Financial Clearing Document

**Tags:** SAP S/4HANA, document clearing, financial accounting

**Prerequisites:** Open-Item Management

**Related:** General Ledger Accounting (FI-GL)

---

#### Reset Clearing

The process of undoing the clearing of open items, allowing reversal of previously cleared documents or correction of incorrectly matched items.

**Also known as:** Clearing Reset, Reset Cleared Items

**Tags:** SAP S/4HANA, financial clearing, document reversal

**Prerequisites:** Cleared Document

**Related:** General Ledger Accounting (FI-GL)

---

#### Posting General Ledger Documents

Posting general ledger documents involves recording financial transactions in SAP that affect general ledger accounts and organizational units.

**Tags:** SAP, finance, general ledger, transaction processing

**Prerequisites:** Posting Keys

**Related:** Document Splitting Steps, Currencies

---

#### Ledger Group Definition

Ledger group definition in SAP groups multiple ledgers for reporting and processing to manage parallel accounting scenarios efficiently.

**Tags:** SAP, finance, accounting, configuration

**Prerequisites:** Configuring Ledgers

**Related:** General Ledger Accounting (FI-GL)

---

#### Maintaining General Ledger Accounts

Maintaining general ledger accounts involves creating, updating, and managing accounts within the chart of accounts to support accurate financial reporting.

**Tags:** SAP, finance, general ledger, accounting

**Prerequisites:** Account Groups

---

#### Open Items

#### Down payment request

A notification sent to a customer requesting an advance payment by the agreed due date, recorded using special general ledger indicator F; the item is deleted once the payment is received.

**Also known as:** Noted item, Down Payment Proposal

**Tags:** financial accounting, payment process, SAP S/4HANA, Special General Ledger, Purchasing, SAP Purchasing, Down Payments, Procurement Process

**Prerequisites:** Special general ledger indicator, FAZ billing type

---

#### Profit center

A profit center is an organizational unit used in accounting to represent areas of responsibility for profit calculation by assigning costs and revenues, often structured within a hierarchy.

**Also known as:** SAP profit center

**Tags:** Accounting, Controlling, Organizational Unit, management accounting, SAP configuration, SAP, Financial Accounting, Segment Reporting, financial reporting, finance, organizational management, SAP S/4HANA, master data, Master Record

#### Payment media creation

The process of generating payment media files in specified formats either simultaneously with the payment run or as a subsequent step by specifying run date, identification, and media format.

**Also known as:** Payment Medium Generation

**Tags:** Accounting, Payments, Payment Process, File Generation, SAP S/4HANA, payment processing, bank communication

**Prerequisites:** Payment medium workbench

**Related:** Payment run

---

#### Representative ledger

In a ledger group, the designated ledger whose posting period status determines whether posting is allowed on all ledgers in that group.

**Tags:** Accounting, Ledger, financial accounting, SAP S/4HANA, ledger group

**Prerequisites:** Ledger group assignment

**Related:** Manage Posting Periods app

---

#### Deactivating a Ledger

The process of disabling a ledger so that it no longer records new transactions, often used during system updates or structural changes.

**Also known as:** Ledger deactivation

**Tags:** Accounting, Ledger Management

**Prerequisites:** Ledger

The accounting process of modifying asset values using either flat-rate or individual adjustments to reflect current value or conditions.

**Prerequisites:** Valuation

#### Balance Carryforward Program

A program executed at fiscal year-end or beginning that transfers account balances from the general ledger, customers, vendors, and asset accounts to the next fiscal year.

#### Posting Journal Document Reversal

The process of reversing an accounting document on the first day of the next period to prevent daily operations from being affected during reconciliation clearing.

**Also known as:** Document Reversal

**Tags:** accounting, document management, financial closing

**Prerequisites:** Goods Receipt/Invoice Receipt Account Clearing

---

#### Delta Posting

Posting where the system records only the amount for the current period without reversing prior postings.

**Tags:** Finance, Accounting, Accrual Posting

**Prerequisites:** Line-item Types

**Related:** Automatic Postings, Periodic Posting

---

#### Complete Posting

Posting where the system reverses prior amounts and posts the entire newly calculated amount.

**Tags:** Finance, Accounting, Accrual Posting

**Prerequisites:** Line-item Types

**Related:** Opening Posting, Closing Posting, Automatic Postings

---

#### Field Status Priorities

The hierarchy of priorities used to resolve conflicts in field statuses between different configuration levels, where 'Suppress' takes highest priority in client level settings, and 'Required' takes highest priority within roles.

**Tags:** SAP S/4HANA, Field Status, Configuration

**Prerequisites:** Business Partner Field Attributes

---

#### Universal Journal Line Items

Detailed ledger entries stored in table ACDOCA after document splitting and ledger-specific line creation, reflecting postings per standard ledger with multiple lines for supplier, expense, and tax.

**Tags:** SAP, Finance, Universal Journal, Accounting

**Prerequisites:** General Ledger Document Posting

---

#### Entry View Document Posting

The initial posting document in SAP before document splitting, typically displaying three posted lines for supplier, expense, and tax, recorded in table BSEG.

**Tags:** SAP, Finance, Document Posting, Reporting

**Prerequisites:** General Ledger Document Posting

---

#### Period Variant

A configuration object defining open and closed posting periods per variant in SAP, controlling when accounting entries can be posted.

**Tags:** SAP, Finance, Period Management

**Prerequisites:** Open and Closed Periods
