---

#### Depreciation Areas

Depreciation areas are segments within a chart of depreciation responsible for calculating asset values according to specific accounting principles and valuation purposes; they control postings to the general ledger.

**Also known as:** Depreciation Segment, Accounting Depreciation Areas

**Tags:** SAP S/4HANA, Asset Accounting, Valuation, depreciation, configuration, Accounting, Finance

**Prerequisites:** Asset Valuation Configuration

**Related:** Real Depreciation Area, Derived Depreciation Areas

---

#### Exchange Rate

The rate used to convert foreign currency amounts into the company code currency during document postings in SAP.

**Also known as:** Currency Exchange Rate

**Tags:** Accounting, Currency Management, SAP S/4HANA

**Prerequisites:** Posting in General Ledger Accounting

---

#### Document Number Range

A set of numbers assigned to documents posted with a specific document type in SAP S/4HANA, defined per company code to ensure unique identification and order.

**Also known as:** Document Number Assignment, document numbering

**Tags:** SAP S/4HANA, General Ledger, Document Management

**Prerequisites:** Posting in General Ledger Accounting

---

#### Business Transaction Variants

More refined classifications within business transactions in SAP allowing specific document splitting rule application per variant.

**Tags:** SAP, accounting, configuration

**Prerequisites:** Active Document Split

---

#### Customizing for Subsequent Implementation of Document Splitting

A set of SAP configuration tasks required to activate document splitting in existing productive systems with postings.

**Also known as:** Document Splitting Subsequent Implementation

**Tags:** SAP, configuration, implementation

**Prerequisites:** Document Splitting Activation

---

#### Primary Cost and Revenue Accounts

Primary cost and revenue accounts capture direct financial postings related to costs and revenues in the general ledger.

**Tags:** SAP, finance, cost accounting, revenue accounting

**Prerequisites:** Maintaining General Ledger Accounts

---

#### SAP S/4HANA Financial Accounting Certification — Application Associate Exam

A professional certification exam that validates an individual's foundational knowledge and skills in SAP S/4HANA Financial Accounting, aimed at application associates responsible for configuring and using the financial accounting modules.

**Also known as:** SAP S/4HANA FI Application Associate Exam, SAP Financial Accounting Certification

**Tags:** Certification, SAP, Finance, Exam Preparation

**Prerequisites:** Financial Accounting Skills

**Related:** Practice Questions for SAP Certification

---

#### Dependency configuration

The setup of task dependencies in SAP Financial Closing Cockpit to define the order and conditions under which closing tasks execute.

**Also known as:** Task dependency configuration

**Tags:** SAP, Workflow, Finance, Financial Closing, Workflow Configuration

**Prerequisites:** Task list, Rules

**Related:** SAP S/4HANA Financial Closing cockpit

---

#### Payment run

The execution process that posts payment documents, clears open items, and accounts for currency gains/losses, taxes, withholding, and discounts based on a finalized payment proposal.

**Also known as:** Automatic Payment Execution

**Tags:** Accounting, Payments, Automation, Payment Process, Finance, SAP S/4HANA

**Prerequisites:** Payment term, Payment block

**Related:** Payment media creation, Outgoing payment, Passive document split

---

#### General Ledger Closing

The set of operations performed to close the general ledger for a fiscal period, including managing posting periods, executing balance carryforward, and audit journal reviews.

**Also known as:** GL Closing

**Tags:** Financial Closing, Financial Accounting, period end closing, SAP S/4HANA

**Prerequisites:** General Ledger Accounting, Posting Period

**Related:** Historical Partition

---

#### Chart of accounts

A structured list of general ledger accounts used in SAP S/4HANA, maintained at the chart of accounts level and assigned to company codes, comprising operational, country/alternative, and group charts.

**Also known as:** COA, Account list

**Tags:** accounting, finance, SAP, Financial Reporting, Financial Accounting, general ledger, accounting structure, SAP S/4HANA, Organizational Structure, accounting master data, master data

**Prerequisites:** Company code, Account Number Length

**Related:** Country chart/accounts, Operational Chart of Accounts, Country/Local Chart of Accounts, Group Account

---

#### Asset depreciation

Asset depreciation is the periodic allocation of an asset’s cost over its useful life, with values calculated and posted automatically in SAP S/4HANA according to configured rules.

**Also known as:** Depreciation, Fixed Asset Depreciation

**Tags:** Asset Accounting, Finance, Depreciation, SAP S/4HANA, Accounting Process

**Prerequisites:** Posting run (Asset Depreciation), Asset acquisition

**Related:** Year-end process, Depreciation key, Transaction, Simulation (Asset Accounting), Low-value assets

---

#### Data Aging Run

A scheduled execution process in SAP that transfers data meeting aging criteria from the hot partition to the cold partition based on defined configuration parameters.

**Also known as:** Aging Run

**Tags:** Data Aging, SAP Jobs, SAP, Data Management, Process Execution

**Prerequisites:** Table Partitioning, Data Aging Group

---

#### Automatic Payment Program

An SAP S/4HANA program designed to manage mass outgoing and incoming payments automatically, supporting domestic, foreign, and intercompany payments with extensive customization.

**Also known as:** APP, Automated Payment

**Tags:** SAP S/4HANA, payments, automation, payment processing, financial accounting

**Prerequisites:** Customizing (Payment Program), Special G/L Transactions to Be Paid / for Exception List

**Related:** Electronic Bank Transfer Files

---

#### Manual Outgoing Payment

A manually posted payment in SAP that clears supplier open items by entering relevant payment and bank data and selecting open items to be cleared.

**Tags:** SAP, payments, supplier accounts, manual processing

**Prerequisites:** Open Items, Accounting Editing Options

**Related:** Payment Document, Individual Payment, Head Office/Branch Accounting

---

#### Manual Incoming Payment

A manually posted payment in SAP that clears customer open items, recorded by entering general information, bank data, and selecting open items to be cleared.

**Tags:** SAP, payments, customer accounts, manual processing

**Prerequisites:** Open Items, Accounting Editing Options

**Related:** Payment Document, Individual Payment, Head Office/Branch Accounting

---

#### Financial Statement Version Item Hierarchy

The multi-level structure (up to 20 levels) within a financial statement version where items are organized in parent-child relationships with subtotal calculations.

**Also known as:** Item Hierarchy

**Tags:** SAP, Financial Statement Version, Hierarchy

**Prerequisites:** Account Assignment to Financial Statement Items, Subdivision of Financial Statement Items

**Related:** Item Keys Auto., Functional Area Perm.

---

#### Financial Accounting Closing Process

The sequence of steps and procedures performed at the end of an accounting period to finalize financial data and prepare statements.

**Also known as:** Financial Closing Process

**Tags:** Financial Closing, Accounting Processes

**Prerequisites:** Balance Sheet Account Carryforward, Profit & Loss (P&L) Account Carryforward

**Related:** Closing Activities for Materials Management, Intercompany Matching and Reconciliation (ICMR), SAP Business Planning and Consolidation (SAP BPC)

---

#### Down payment

An advance amount received from a customer, recorded with special general ledger indicator A, which replaces the down payment request and is later cleared as a credit open item against the invoice.

**Tags:** financial accounting, payment process, SAP S/4HANA, Purchasing

**Prerequisites:** Special general ledger indicator, Down payment request

**Related:** Credit open item

---

#### Asset Master Record

A record in SAP Asset Accounting containing all relevant information and parameters for a particular asset, used for posting acquisitions, retirements, and depreciation.

**Also known as:** Asset Record, Fixed Asset Master Record, Fixed Asset Record

**Tags:** Asset Accounting, SAP S/4HANA, Master Data, SAP, Asset Management, Data Records

**Prerequisites:** Data Migration (Asset Accounting), Asset Accounting Organizational Units

**Related:** Asset Subnumbers, Maximum Value for Asset in LVA Class, Settlement (Asset Accounting)

---

#### Answer All Questions Strategy

An approach advocating answering every question, as there is no penalty for wrong answers in SAP certification exams, making educated guesses beneficial.

**Also known as:** Complete Answering, Attempt Every Question

**Tags:** exam strategy

**Prerequisites:** No Penalty for Wrong Answers, Educated Guessing

---

#### Dunning Levels

Defined stages within a dunning procedure characterized by criteria such as days overdue, interest calculation, and printing options; they determine the escalation steps in dunning.

**Also known as:** Dunning Stages

**Tags:** SAP, Dunning, Process Configuration

**Prerequisites:** Number of Dunning Levels, Days in Arrears for Dunning Level

**Related:** Dunning Even for Credit Account Balance, Standard Dunning Procedures, Total Due Items from Dunning Level, Calculate Interest Flag, Always Dun Flag, Public Holiday Calendar ID, Blocked Items for Dunning

---

#### Business Partner Role Assignment

The process of assigning one or more roles to a business partner to define the nature of business relations and control relevant fields for each role.

**Tags:** SAP S/4HANA, Master Data, Business Partner

**Prerequisites:** Master Data Creation, Role Grouping Functionality

**Related:** Supplier Role, Custom Business Partner Role

---

#### SAP S/4HANA for Financial Accounting Associates Certification (C_TS4FI_2020)

A certification validating foundational knowledge and skills in financial accounting processes using SAP S/4HANA, targeted at new consultants and professionals entering SAP financials.

**Also known as:** C_TS4FI_2020, SAP S/4HANA Financial Accounting Certification

**Tags:** Certification, SAP, Financial Accounting, ERP

**Prerequisites:** Financial Accounting, Implementation and Support Consultants

---

#### Rules for Changing Document Header and Line Items

Configurations defining which fields in the document header and line items can be changed after posting, varying by company code, account type, and transaction type.

**Also known as:** Change Control Rules

**Tags:** SAP S/4HANA, Document Management, Accounting

**Prerequisites:** Changing Documents, Field Status Definitions

---

#### Asset Acquisition with Purchase Order Integrated with Materials Management

The most common asset acquisition method involving purchase order processing with materials management, where acquisition postings are completed through invoice verification and may include valuated goods receipts.

**Also known as:** PO-Based Asset Acquisition

**Tags:** Asset Acquisition, SAP S/4HANA, Materials Management, Purchase Order

**Prerequisites:** Fixed Assets, Purchase Order (PO)

**Related:** Accounting-Principle-Specific Document

---

#### Depreciation posting

The periodic accounting process performed during period-end closing that records the calculated depreciation amounts of assets in the asset accounting component.

**Tags:** depreciation, accounting process, period-end closing

**Prerequisites:** Calculation methods for depreciation, Account Determination, Header Segment (Document Posting)

---

#### Organizational units in financial accounting

Entities like company code, business area, segment, and functional area that form part of the enterprise structure for financial accounting purposes in SAP.

**Tags:** SAP, Organizational structure, Financial Accounting

**Prerequisites:** Organizational units (in SAP), Copying Company Code, Workflow variant (in Financial Accounting)

**Related:** Purchasing organization

---

### Level 3 - Advanced

#### Test Run for Depreciation Posting

A preliminary execution of the depreciation posting run that simulates postings to identify errors before the actual posting run is committed.

**Also known as:** Depreciation Simulation Run

**Tags:** asset accounting, process, testing

**Prerequisites:** Depreciation posting

---

#### Group-level Summarized Amount

A calculated subtotal for financial statement items aggregating account balances at and below a given hierarchy node.

**Also known as:** Graduated Total

**Tags:** SAP, Financial Reporting, Calculations

**Prerequisites:** Financial Statement Version Item Hierarchy

---

#### Certification Exam - Financial Closing Topic

Assessment component testing knowledge and skills related to the financial accounting closing activities within SAP S/4HANA, comprising about 15% of the exam.

**Also known as:** SAP Certification - Financial Closing

**Tags:** SAP Certification, Financial Closing, Examination

**Prerequisites:** Financial Accounting Closing Process

---

#### Value Maintenance

Value maintenance settings define allowed value types and rules for different valuations within depreciation areas for fixed assets in SAP S/4HANA.

**Also known as:** Valuation Rules

**Tags:** SAP S/4HANA, Asset Accounting, Configuration

**Prerequisites:** Depreciation Areas

---

#### Translation Date

The date used by SAP to determine the applicable exchange rate for currency translation during document posting.

**Tags:** Accounting, Currency Management, SAP S/4HANA

**Prerequisites:** Exchange Rate

---

#### Cross-Company-Code Transaction Posting

The process of posting general ledger entries that involve multiple company codes within a single document.

**Also known as:** Intercompany Posting

**Tags:** Accounting, SAP S/4HANA, General Ledger

**Prerequisites:** Document Number Range

---

#### Tax Account Determination

The process in SAP S/4HANA determining which general ledger tax accounts are used for tax postings based on tax type account keys and configured accounts.

**Tags:** SAP configuration, accounting, tax accounting

**Prerequisites:** Account Key, Tax Type

---

#### Account Currency

The currency assigned to a general ledger account at the company code level which restricts or permits posting in multiple currencies depending on whether it matches the company code currency.

**Tags:** Accounting, SAP, Currency Management, Financial Accounting, Currency, Finance, Master Data

**Prerequisites:** Company Code Level Maintenance, Currency Key

---

### Level 4 - Expert

#### Posting Tax Accounts

Rules defining how tax amounts are posted in SAP, either as separate line items or distributed among relevant revenue or expense accounts, such as nondeductible taxes.

**Tags:** accounting, tax postings, SAP

**Prerequisites:** Tax Account Determination

---

### Level 5 - Specialized

#### Document Posting

The SAP process of entering a financial document with a header (global details) and line items (detailed entries) for general ledger accounting.

**Also known as:** Posting Journal Entries

**Tags:** SAP accounting, financial posting, ERP, finance, SAP S/4HANA, transaction

**Prerequisites:** Field Status Group, Posting Tax Accounts, Materials Management Account Determination

---
